### I.4.F — Sequencing

Sequence I.4 *after* I.2 Daily Statement lands. Rationale: I.2 sets the good example (greenfield datasets with no exclusions); I.4 retrofits existing AR datasets to match. Doing I.4 first would delay the higher-value I.2 work and complicate the Daily Statement's own test inventory.

Estimated 2–4 commits. If I.4.B/C grows past that (because removing exclusions uncovers visual regressions requiring redesign), promote to its own Phase J entry and leave a smaller I.4 behind.

## I.5 — PR sign convention standardization (merchant_dda balance reflects actual flow)

**North star.** PR merchant_dda accounts should follow the same sign convention as the rest of the codebase: `signed_amount > 0` = money IN to the account; `signed_amount < 0` = money OUT; `daily_balances.balance = SUM(signed_amount)` reflects what the merchant actually has on hand. Surfaced during I.4.B Commit 1 — the PR generator emits `payment` outflow legs on merchant_dda accounts but no compensating inbound, because the sale leg also debits merchant_sub (backwards from convention). This forces PR datasets to negate signed_amount in 6+ places (`-t.signed_amount AS amount`) to recover positive display values. I.5 fixes both: align the seed signs AND retire the negation pattern in PR datasets.

Why a standalone phase rather than a sub-step of I.4: the fix touches generator + datasets + tests + likely visuals; SHA256 re-lock will shift many PR e2e expectations; the diff is broad enough to deserve its own commit cadence and review surface. I.4 stays focused on filter removal; I.5 owns the sign convention.

### I.5.A — Audit current PR sign usage

- [x] **Generator inventory.** Mapped (2026-04-20). Sale leg at `demo_data.py:384-387` was the bug; settlement leg kept self-cancelling (logical grouping, no money actually moves; the payment leg already does the cash-out movement); payment leg unchanged (correct under the new convention). No other PR-side `_posting` sites touched merchant_sub or `pr-external-*` with a wrong sign.
- [x] **Dataset inventory.** Mapped (2026-04-20). Three sites carried `-t.signed_amount` or `SUM(-signed_amount)` in `payment_recon/datasets.py`: `build_sales_dataset` (~L323), `build_settlement_exceptions_dataset` (~L436), `build_sale_settlement_mismatch_dataset` (~L501). All three were "absolute display value" recoveries — none carried semantic intent — so all three retire to plain `t.signed_amount` / `SUM(signed_amount)` after the generator flip.
- [x] **Test inventory.** Mapped (2026-04-20). Two PR tests negated signed_amount on the read path: `tests/test_demo_data.py` recovery in two scenario tests (L348, L359) and `tests/e2e/test_pr_kpi_semantics.py` (L148 comment + L166 SUM probe). Both updated in I.5.B+C+D bundle commit.
- [x] **`_ACH_ORIG_CUSTOMERS` parallel check.** Decided (2026-04-20) it's a SEPARATE issue — not a sign convention bug, but a missing-counter-flow seed shape (customer DDAs only see ACH outflow with no inbound). Stays AR-side; out of scope for I.5.
- [x] **Document the target convention.** Done in I.5.F.

### I.5.B — Generator-side sign correction

- [x] **Sale leg flip.** Done in commit c121869 (I.5.B+C+D bundle). `demo_data.py:384-387` now emits merchant_sub `+sale["amount"]`, `pr-external-customer-pool` `-sale["amount"]`.
- [x] **Settlement leg revisit.** Decided (2026-04-20) to keep self-cancelling — settlement is a logical grouping in this model; the payment leg already moves the money. No change to demo_data.py here.
- [x] **Payment leg verify.** Verified unchanged; merchant_sub `-payment_amount` is correct under the new convention.
- [x] **Determinism.** SHA256 re-locked to `6912a28c8902223a7a552194ee368f1e83df09d6779e5c735321a83c086c1cf0` in `tests/test_demo_data.py::TestDeterminism::test_seed_output_hash_is_locked`. AR seed unchanged at this stage.
- [ ] **Sign-convention contract test.** Deferred — the new I.5.E inverse assertion (no merchant_dda is structurally negative for the seed window) achieves the same regression guard one level up. Reopen if a future regression slips through that gap.
- [ ] **Balance-coherence test.** Deferred — same gap is covered by I.5.E.

### I.5.C — Dataset cleanup (retire `-t.signed_amount` pattern)

- [x] Retired in commit c121869: 3 sites in `payment_recon/datasets.py` (`build_sales_dataset`, `build_settlement_exceptions_dataset`, `build_sale_settlement_mismatch_dataset`) and the matching ETL example in `payment_recon/etl_examples.py` (Pattern 1 sale).
- [x] DatasetContract types unchanged — all three sites kept DECIMAL.
- [x] `tests/test_dataset_contract.py` unchanged — column expectations didn't shift.

### I.5.D — Test re-lock and fallout

- [x] Done in commit c121869. SHA256 re-locked. PR e2e tests: `tests/e2e/test_pr_kpi_semantics.py` had one SUM probe + one comment to flip; both updated. Unit tests: 398 pass. PR Settlement / Payment Mismatch checks — unchanged as predicted (read on transfer_id grouping, not per-leg sign). No other test required a hardcoded-value flip.

### I.5.E — Cross-visibility regression update

- [x] Done in commit 4bb6122. `test_merchant_dda_overdrafts_surface` rewritten as `test_no_merchant_dda_is_structurally_negative` (inverse assertion — locks the I.5 fix). Cross-visibility itself stays locked by the view-definition test in the sibling class.
- [x] Test docstrings updated to reference "Phase I.5 — sign convention standardization."

### I.5.F — Docs + sequencing

- [x] CLAUDE.md: added a **Sign convention** paragraph immediately after the shared base layer table bullets — `signed_amount > 0` = money IN, `< 0` = OUT, `daily_balances.balance = SUM(signed_amount)`, applies to every account_type including merchant_dda. Inline parenthetical on the `transactions` bullet now uses the same account-holder phrasing.
- [x] `docs/Schema_v3.md`: column-spec entry updated; new **Sign convention** subsection right after Indexes reconciles the bank's-bookkeeping reading ("+= debit") with the account-holder reading ("= money IN") — same statement, opposite ends of the double-entry. ETL walkthrough `how-do-i-populate-transactions.md:133` got the same treatment.
- [x] PR Handbook spot-check: no "merchant balance is structurally negative" language existed in PR walkthroughs (grep confirmed). No edits needed.
- [x] Sequencing held — I.5 followed I.4 as planned.
- [x] Final cadence: 3 commits (I.5.B+C+D bundle, I.5.E, I.5.F docs), well under the 4–6 estimate.

## I.6 — Release to PyPI + GitHub release artifacts

**North star.** `pip install quicksight-gen[demo]` works from PyPI on any tagged release. A GitHub Release page accompanies each tag with the wheel, sdist, and a pre-baked sample `out/` bundle so evaluators can inspect generated QuickSight JSON without running the generator. Tag-triggered workflow does the build, smoke-test against the wheel, publish, and release-notes draft.

**Why now.** The repo is past v3.0.0 in RELEASE_NOTES (Phase G shipped) but `pyproject.toml` still says `1.1.0`. Anyone who wants to use the tool today has to clone + `pip install -e .` — there's no `pip install`-from-PyPI path. Setting up the release pipeline now establishes the cadence; later phases can ship with a single tag push.

### I.6.A — Version source-of-truth audit + sync

- [x] **Reconcile version.** Aligned `pyproject.toml` *up* to the RELEASE_NOTES.md track (was 1.1.0, now reads 3.0.0 from the dynamic source) — single-line change vs. renaming a dozen historical RELEASE_NOTES headers. Future bumps proceed from 3.0.0; phase-major (4.0.0) for schema/semantic changes, phase-minor (3.1.0) for additive features.
- [x] **Single source of truth.** `src/quicksight_gen/__init__.py` carries `__version__`; `pyproject.toml` reads it via `[tool.setuptools.dynamic] version = {attr = "quicksight_gen.__version__"}`. Verified `pip install -e .` + `pip show quicksight-gen` + `import quicksight_gen` all agree.
- [x] **Document the bump-then-tag sequence** in CLAUDE.md (release section). → Done as part of I.6.G; the version flag + README snippet make the workflow self-documenting (`bump __version__ → commit → tag → push tag`).

### I.6.B — Release-readiness audit on `pyproject.toml`

- [x] **Classifiers.** Added Development Status (Beta), Intended Audience (Developers + Financial), OS Independent, Python 3 / 3.11 / 3.12 / 3.13, Topic Office/Business/Financial/Accounting + Code Generators. License classifier omitted in favor of SPDX `license = "Unlicense"` (PEP 639).
- [x] **URLs.** `[project.urls]` carries Homepage + Documentation (mkdocs site), Source, Issues, Changelog (RELEASE_NOTES.md on main).
- [x] **README rendering.** `readme = "README.md"`; `twine check dist/*` PASSED for both wheel + sdist.
- [x] **Keywords.** `quicksight`, `aws`, `dashboards`, `reconciliation`, `analytics`, `finance`.
- [x] **Package data.** Wheel ships `quicksight_gen/` (including `quicksight_gen/demo/schema.sql`, declared via `[tool.setuptools.package-data]`). Sdist ships README + LICENSE + pyproject + src/ + tests/. `quicksight-gen demo schema --all -o <path>` reads the schema through `quicksight_gen.demo.generate_schema_sql()` (`importlib.resources` lookup) so it works against an installed wheel. *(Originally claimed `demo schema` "generated" the SQL; it actually ships the static file via package-data — corrected in v3.2.1.)*

### I.6.C — Local build + smoke test

- [x] **`python -m build`.** Produces `dist/quicksight_gen-3.0.0.tar.gz` + `quicksight_gen-3.0.0-py3-none-any.whl`. `build` + `twine` added to `[project.optional-dependencies].dev`.
- [x] **Fresh-venv install.** `/tmp/qs-smoke` venv installs the wheel cleanly; `quicksight-gen --help` shows all 4 subcommands (cleanup, demo, deploy, generate). `--version` flag deferred to I.6.G alongside the README badge.
- [x] **`generate --all` smoke.** Against a minimal config (no real ARNs), the wheel-installed CLI produces all 39 expected output files (theme + 4 analysis/dashboard JSONs + 34 datasets). Confirms no package-data files were forgotten.
- [x] **`twine check dist/*`.** PASSED for both wheel + sdist (long-description renders on PyPI).

### I.6.D — PyPI account + trusted publishing setup

- [x] **TestPyPI first.** Trusted Publisher configured; v3.2.1 + v3.2.2 published to TestPyPI via OIDC.
- [x] **PyPI.** Trusted Publisher configured; v3.2.1 published to PyPI on 2026-04-20.
- [x] **GitHub Environments.** `testpypi` + `pypi` environments created; `pypi` has manual approval gate.
- [x] **No API tokens in repo secrets.** Pure OIDC end-to-end; verified by inspecting the workflow runs.

### I.6.E — Release workflow (`.github/workflows/release.yml`)

- [x] **Trigger.** `on: push: tags: ['v[0-9]+.[0-9]+.[0-9]+']` (excludes pre-release suffixes; add `'v[0-9]+.[0-9]+.[0-9]+-*'` later for rc / beta tags if needed). Concurrency group keyed on tag prevents overlapping runs.
- [x] **Job: build.** `pypa/build` produces sdist + wheel; `twine check` confirms long-description renders; tag-vs-`__version__` mismatch fails the job up front. Uploads `dist/` as a workflow artifact.
- [x] **Job: smoke.** Downloads the wheel artifact, installs into a fresh venv with the test extras, asserts `quicksight-gen --version` echoes the tag, runs the unit + integration test subset (`test_models / test_account_recon / test_demo_data / test_demo_sql / test_recon / test_generate / test_theme_presets / test_dataset_contract`).
- [x] **Job: bake-sample.** Downloads the wheel, installs into a separate fresh venv, runs `scripts/bake_sample_output.py`, uploads `dist/out-sample.zip` as a workflow artifact for the release job.
- [x] **Job: publish-testpypi.** Always on tag; environment `testpypi` (Trusted Publisher OIDC); depends on `smoke` + `bake-sample`.
- [x] **Job: publish-pypi.** Gated on `publish-testpypi` success + manual approval on the `pypi` environment; Trusted Publisher OIDC.
- [x] **Job: github-release.** `softprops/action-gh-release@v2`; release body extracted from `RELEASE_NOTES.md` via `awk` (matches `## v{tag}` heading, stops at the next `---`); uploads sdist + wheel + `out-sample.zip` with `fail_on_unmatched_files: true`.

### I.6.F — Sample output bundle

- [x] **`scripts/bake_sample_output.py`** — runs `python -m quicksight_gen generate --all` against `examples/config.yaml` into a temp dir, zips to `dist/out-sample.zip` with the `out/` prefix preserved. Local smoke produced 39 entries, 86 KB.
- [x] **`examples/config.yaml`** — placeholder ARNs (account `111122223333`, region `us-east-1`, theme `sasquatch-bank`); demo URL commented out. Lives at repo root; **does not ship in the wheel** — the sample bundle on each GitHub Release is the artifact evaluators consume, and source-from-GitHub callers find it under `examples/`. Re-evaluate if friction emerges.

### I.6.G — README + badges

- [x] **PyPI install snippet** — `## Quick start` now leads with `### Install from PyPI` (consumer path) before `### Setup from source` (developer path). `pip install quicksight-gen` for ARN-only callers, `pip install "quicksight-gen[demo]"` for demo mode.
- [x] **PyPI version badge** added alongside CI + Coverage. Will read "no releases" until first publish, then live.
- [x] **`quicksight-gen --version` flag.** Wired via `click.version_option(version=__version__, prog_name="quicksight-gen")`. Reports the dynamic version from `quicksight_gen.__version__`.

### I.6.H — Sequencing

- [x] **Independent of I.4 / I.5.** Held as planned — first cut went out after I.5's SHA256 re-lock landed.
- [x] **First release flow.** Actual sequence: v3.2.0 (smoke failed on schema-not-in-wheel) → v3.2.1 fix (TestPyPI → PyPI → GitHub Release, all green) → v3.2.2 (refactor: schema is interface contract, not demo). Pipeline validated end-to-end.
- [x] **Estimated 6–8 commits.** Actual commit count for I.6: 8 commits across A/B/C/E/F/G + 2 release-followups (v3.2.1 + v3.2.2). Within estimate.

### I.6.I — Open questions

- [x] **Pre-release channel.** Do branch builds publish to TestPyPI automatically (e.g., on push to a `release/*` branch with a `v1.6.0-rc1`-style tag), or only formal tags? Recommend formal-tags-only initially; revisit if the cadence picks up.
- [x] **Package name on PyPI.** `quicksight-gen` is the natural name (matches `[project].name`) — verify availability on PyPI before I.6.D registration. If taken, fall back to `quicksight-generator` or namespaced (`anthropic-quicksight-gen` style) — bigger renames flow back through `[project.scripts]` and `__init__.py`.
- [x] **License clarity.** `Unlicense` is public domain; PyPI accepts it. Confirm the `LICENSE` file at repo root matches and is included in the wheel (`tool.setuptools.license-files` defaults usually pick it up).

## Schema cleanup carry-over from Phase G

-- [x] ~~**PR-coexistence filters in AR views**~~ — *resolved by Phase I.4.B (commits 1–4).* The original entry assumed the future was PR/AR *separation* (delete the filters, a single-feed persona has no parallel PR ledger). I.4 flipped that: AR is the superset; PR is a subset view. The artificial filters were removed in I.4.B commits 1–3; commit 4 updated CLAUDE.md / SPEC.md / RELEASE_NOTES.md to match.
- ~~**AR drift views leak benign zero-drift PR rows**~~ — *resolved by Phase I.4.B commit 1.* Both `account_id NOT LIKE 'pr-%'` filters dropped from `ar_subledger_overdraft` and `ar_subledger_daily_outbound_by_type`. Drift views now expose merchant DDA rows by intent.
- [x] **Unified account dimension table.** AR currently keeps `ar_ledger_accounts` and `ar_subledger_accounts` as separate dimension tables. A single "all accounts" table aligns with the denormalize-don't-add-tables north star and would simplify some queries. Low priority; ship when there's a query that benefits.

# PLAN — Phase J (queued)

## Customer-facing customization handbook

- [ ] `docs/Schema_v3.md` is the persona contract for the Data Integration Team. A longer-form customer-facing customization guide (mapping production-system tables → the two base tables, common pitfalls, performance tips, replacing dataset SQL while preserving DatasetContract) is a natural follow-up to the demo-side walkthroughs in Phase H. Deliverable shape: a "Customization Handbook" sibling to AR / PR Handbooks.

### Outline (drafted 2026-04-20 for review)

**Audience.** Developers / product owners reshaping the product onto their own backend — *not* the Data Integration ETL engineer (that's the existing Data Integration Handbook). Per SPEC.md "Users" section.

**Anchored at the contract level — explicitly NOT covering:** per-visual customization (visuals will rework under Phase K persona redesigns), per-dataset SQL enumeration (32+ datasets and growing), per-sheet layout (likely to split per-persona). The handbook documents stable surfaces: the two-table contract, the DatasetContract pattern, metadata JSON, theme presets, config + CLI.

**Placement.** `docs/handbook/customization.md` (overview) + `docs/walkthroughs/customization/*.md` per topic. Add fourth handbook section to `mkdocs.yml` nav after Data Integration.

**Walkthroughs:**

- [x] **J.0 — Handbook overview page.** `docs/handbook/customization.md` + `mkdocs.yml` nav entry. Audience framing, "what stays stable across persona changes" intro, card grid linking to J.1–J.8.
- [x] **J.1 — How do I map my production database to the two base tables?** Pattern-level mapping (not per-system enumeration); cross-link to `walkthroughs/etl/how-do-i-populate-transactions.md` for the ETL-engineer view.
- [x] **J.2 — How do I swap the SQL behind a dataset without breaking the visuals?** DatasetContract (column name + type list) is the binding contract; show the contract test that locks projection-vs-contract; point at `common/dataset_contract.py`.
- [x] **J.3 — How do I reskin the dashboards for my brand?** Theme preset pattern (`common/theme.py` PRESETS registry), color tokens (accent / primary_fg / link_tint), `analysis_name_prefix` for demo-vs-prod naming.
- [x] **J.4 — How do I configure the deploy for my AWS account?** `config.yaml` fields (account / region / resource_prefix / principal_arns / extra_tags / theme_preset / late_default_days), production `datasource_arn` vs demo `demo_database_url`, env-var override pattern (`QS_GEN_*`).
- [x] **J.5 — How do I run my first deploy?** `quicksight-gen deploy --all --generate`, idempotent delete-then-create, `cleanup --dry-run` before `--yes`, `ManagedBy` tagging.
- [x] **J.6 — How do I add an app-specific metadata key?** Cross-link to `walkthroughs/etl/how-do-i-add-a-metadata-key.md` (the ETL angle is identical — same `JSON_VALUE` pattern); customization angle adds: where to read it in dataset SQL, when to surface as a column vs filter.
- [x] **J.7 — How do I extend the schema with a new transfer_type or account_type value?** Conventions for adding to the canonical value lists; downstream impact (filter dropdowns auto-expand, no new tables needed).
- [x] **J.8 — How do I run the test suite against my customized dataset SQL?** pytest layout, `DatasetContract` assertions, when to add an e2e test vs a unit test.

**Sequencing.** Independent of Phase K persona work — the contract surfaces this handbook documents are exactly the ones that *don't* churn under persona additions, so writing now doesn't create rework risk. Estimated 1 overview + 8 walkthroughs ≈ 9 commits, mostly prose.

# PLAN - Phase K (Shipped)

- **K.1 — AR Exceptions workflow split + handbook rewrite + MIT relicense.** Released in **v3.5.0** (with v3.5.1 / v3.5.2 follow-ups for CI hardening + SLSA build provenance). Today's Exceptions (unified-table operational view) + Exceptions Trends (rollups + aging matrix + per-check daily trend) replaced the dense single Exceptions tab. 17 walkthroughs rewritten, 22 fresh screenshots, mkdocs nav switched to horizontal tabs, license switched from Unlicense to MIT. See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.
- **K.2 — Cross-sheet drill parameter hygiene + typed helpers.** Released in **v3.6.0** (with v3.6.1 doc patch — see below). All six AR drill `FilterGroup`s switched from parameter-bound `CategoryFilter`s (which silently match the empty-string sentinel and suppress every row) to a calc-field PASS shape. New `common/drill.py` introduces `ColumnShape` + `DrillParam` + `DrillSourceField` + `cross_sheet_drill()` that refuse a wiring whose source-field shape can't assign to the destination param's expected shape — fails at the buggy line, not in a downstream output-walking test. All 13 drill sites (7 PR + 6 AR) migrated; the 4 AR drills into Transactions auto-reset every PASS-filtered param the caller doesn't write. `ar_unified_exceptions` became a `MATERIALIZED VIEW` so Today's Exceptions renders under Direct Query. See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.
- **K.2.6 doc follow-up — `ar_unified_exceptions` matview refresh contract.** Released in **v3.6.1**. New "Materialized views" section in `docs/Schema_v3.md` (sits between *Computed views catalogue* and *ETL examples*) listing the view, the `REFRESH MATERIALIZED VIEW` requirement after each ETL load, the timing semantics for `days_outstanding` / `aging_bucket` (computed at refresh time, so skipping a refresh lags the analyst-facing aging), and a "when to materialize the next view" rule. Cross-link added from `docs/handbook/etl.md`. v3.6.0 had wired the REFRESH into `demo apply` but never wrote the contract down for production ETL teams; v3.6.1 fixes that. Docs only — no code changes.
- **K.2a — Identifier scatter cleanup (typed constants for opaque IDs).** Released in **v3.7.0**. Six commits land the same "encode invariants in the type system" approach K.2 took for drill shapes, but applied to the rest of the identifier surface. K.2a.1 promoted all 118 `fg-ar-*` / `fg-pr-*` filter group ID literals to `FG_*` constants; K.2a.2 added `P_PR_SETTLEMENT_ID` / `P_PR_PAYMENT_ID` / `P_PR_EXTERNAL_TXN_ID` mirroring `P_AR_*`; K.2a.3 swept all 314 visual ID literals into `V_*` constants (catches the silent `SheetVisualScopingConfigurations.VisualIds` typo class — a typo there mis-scopes a filter without raising); K.2a.4 wrapped each constant family in a `NewType` (`SheetId`, `VisualId`, `FilterGroupId`, `ParameterName`) so call-site signatures cross-check the *kind* of string, not just `str`. K.2a.5 introduced a `DemoPersona` dataclass in `common/persona.py` as the single source of truth for whitelabel-substitutable strings (institution name, "Fed", `gl-1010` family, account labels, merchants, flavor terms); `training/mapping.yaml.example` is now auto-derived via `derive_mapping_yaml_text()` and a parity test prints the regenerated body when they diverge — so a merchant rename can no longer silently de-sync the publish-time substitution map. K.2a.5b closed the last bare-string hole on AWS enum-like fields (`ElementType`, `CrossDataset`, `Status`, `Scope`, `Trigger`) by switching their dataclass annotations from `str` to `Literal[...]` and adding `ClassVar` constants on the bearing model (`GridLayoutElement.VISUAL`, `FilterGroup.SINGLE_DATASET`, etc.). No analysis, dataset, or runtime behavior change — type-system-only refactor; the new constants module + `DemoPersona` dataclass + `Literal` annotations are the public-facing diff. See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.
- **K.3 — Lateness as a data column, not an operator threshold.** Released in **v3.8.0**. Five sub-phases land the move from PR's `late_default_days` slider math to a per-leg `expected_complete_at TIMESTAMP NULL` on `transactions` plus a downstream `is_late` STRING (`"Late" / "On Time"`) projection; the column is optional with a `posted_at + INTERVAL '1 day'` COALESCE fallback so existing ETL keeps working. K.3.0 added the schema column + the "Lateness as data" section in `Schema_v3.md` (with the multi-leg tie-breaker rule — earliest debit leg's `expected_complete_at` becomes the transfer-level deadline) + the ETL-handbook population-guidance section. K.3.1 populated `expected_complete_at` per rail in both demo generators (PR: card payments T+3, external_txn +1h; AR: instant rails same-day, ACH T+2; everything else NULL) and re-locked both per-app SHA256 seed-hashes. K.3.2 added `is_late` + `expected_complete_at` columns to `ar_unified_exceptions`, the relevant per-check views, and 6 PR exception/recon datasets via a shared `_lateness_columns()` helper; PR's recon dataset switched `match_status` from the operator-threshold pattern to deriving from the same `is_late` predicate. K.3.3 added a Lateness picker on AR Today's Exceptions + Trends (new `fg-ar-todays-exc-is-late` filter group + cross-sheet controls), surfaced `is_late` on the unified exceptions table, updated PR's Late Transactions KPI subtitle to data-driven phrasing, and **fully retired** the `cfg.late_default_days` field + `QS_GEN_LATE_DEFAULT_DAYS` env var — no fallback, no shim, per the project's "no backward-compat hacks" rule. K.3.4 rewrote the PR `why-is-this-external-transaction-unmatched` walkthrough's demo-data + interpretation sections around the rail-hour deadline (most unmatched externals now `match_status='late'`; orphan-recent vs orphan-late reframed as urgency tiers via aging buckets), added an "Optional ETL extensions" section to `handbook/customization.md` introducing `expected_complete_at` alongside `metadata`, and cross-linked the Lateness-as-data anchor from both AR and PR handbook Reference lists. K.3.5 published as v3.8.0 (minor — additive schema, contract gains a column). See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.
- **K.4 — Investigation app (third app: AML + general investigation) + `apps/` namespace re-org.** Released in **v4.0.0** (major). Adds the Investigation app — AML / compliance triage, the third QuickSight app alongside PR + AR — sharing the existing two-table base layer with no schema change. K.4.0 was a Sankey feasibility spike (passed; recursive CTE → QuickSight native Sankey works on PR's existing `parent_transfer_id` chains). K.4.1 was the breaking-change re-org — `payment_recon/` + `account_recon/` moved into `quicksight_gen.apps.*` (no compat shims, old paths raise `ModuleNotFoundError`); the obsolete `training/distribute.py` + `training/publish.py` modules (superseded by `quicksight-gen export training` since v3.4.0) were deleted. K.4.2 stood up the app skeleton + `sasquatch-bank-investigation` theme preset + CLI wiring. K.4.3 – K.4.5 built the three core sheets in feasibility order: Recipient Fanout (straight aggregation; recipient pool filtered to customer / merchant DDAs only so administrative sweeps don't dominate the ranking), Volume Anomalies (matview `inv_pair_rolling_anomalies` — rolling 2-day SUM per (sender, recipient) + population mean / sample stddev → per-row z-score + 5-band bucket label, σ filter scoped `SELECTED_VISUALS` so the distribution chart sees the full population), and Money Trail (matview `inv_money_trail_edges` — `WITH RECURSIVE` walk over `parent_transfer_id` flattened to one row per multi-leg edge with chain root + depth + `source_display` / `target_display` strings; native QuickSight Sankey + hop-by-hop table side-by-side). K.4.6 planted three converging demo scenarios on Juniper Ridge LLC (12-depositor fanout cluster + Cascadia Trust Bank $25K spike vs $300–$700 baseline + 4-hop layering chain through three shell DDAs) so each sheet has a non-empty answer; investigation registers its own internal + external ledger sub-tree so `demo seed investigation` is FK-safe standalone. K.4.7 investigated cross-app drills (Investigation → AR/PR via URL deep-link), built the `CustomActionURLOperation` model + `cross_app_drill()` helper, wired three deferred drills, then **dropped the feature** — QuickSight doesn't sync sheet parameter controls to URL-set values; data filters but the on-screen widgets stay "All". Same defect affects QS's own Navigation Action; re-entry conditions documented in PLAN.md tech debt. K.4.8 added Account Network as a fifth sheet — second view over the K.4.5 matview, account-anchored instead of chain-rooted, with two side-by-side directional Sankeys (inbound on the left + outbound on the right + anchor visually meeting in the middle) + walk-the-flow drill (right-click table row + left-click Sankey node both overwrite `pInvANetworkAnchor` with the counterparty); the K.4.5 + K.4.8 anchor dropdowns gained `Visibility = HIDDEN` on the All entry so QS lands on the first row at first paint, and K.4.8k added a tiny dedicated dropdown-source dataset (`inv-anetwork-accounts-ds`) that pre-deduplicates display strings so the dropdown opens fast as the matview grows. K.4.9 added 28 browser e2e tests across 6 modules (mirroring AR's coverage shape — deployed-resources, dashboard structure, dashboard renders, sheet visuals, filters, drilldown); 3 tests deferred for DOM follow-up (URL-hash parameter pre-seeding breaks dashboard loading, walk-action witness needs to be more reliable than touching-edges row count). K.4.10 added the Investigation handbook + 4 walkthroughs (one per sheet's question), framing the app as **question-shaped** vs. PR's pipeline-staged or AR's rotation-driven; mkdocs nav + `index.md` updated to count three apps. K.4.11 published as v4.0.0 (major — breaking import path changes + new app + new matviews + REFRESH contract additions). See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.

# PLAN - Phase L (Shipped)

Phase L's headline: replaced the constant-heavy, manually-cross-referenced dashboard construction in `apps/{payment_recon,account_recon,investigation}/{analysis,filters,visuals}.py` with a tree of typed builder objects in `common/tree/`. Each app composes top-down — `App → Dashboard / Analysis → Sheet → (Parameters | FilterGroups | Visuals | Controls)` — with cross-references resolved via object refs (FilterGroup scope refers to a Visual node, drill destinations refer to Sheet nodes, etc.) instead of string IDs. The existing `models.py` dataclasses stay as the JSON-emission layer. Released as **v5.0.2** (major — internal API change; external callers importing `quicksight_gen.apps.*.{analysis,filters,visuals}` for programmatic dashboard construction need to migrate to `quicksight_gen.common.tree`). v5.0.0 + v5.0.1 cut + cancelled per the project's "every failed release attempt earns a new version number" policy — both attempts surfaced release-pipeline reliability gaps that landed as part of v5.0.2.

The three-layer model surfaced as the load-bearing design: **L1** (`common/tree/`, `common/models.py`, `common/ids.py`, `common/dataset_contract.py`) — persona-blind primitives; **L2** (`apps/<app>/app.py`) — per-app tree assembly speaking domain vocabulary; **L3** (`apps/<app>/datasets.py` SQL strings, `demo_data.py`, `common/persona.py`, theme presets) — persona / customer flavor. The tree's existence was the test case for the layer separation: anything Sasquatch-specific that leaks into L1 means the API isn't right yet (codified as an ongoing grep invariant).

- **L.0 — Tree spike (`spike/l-tree-account-network`).** Smallest possible port to validate the L1 primitives produced JSON the existing `models.py` accepts. **Result: byte-identical Account Network sheet on first run.** Spike's four primitives (`SheetNode`, `VisualNode`, `ParameterControlNode`, `GridSlot`) and the object-ref + `emit()` pattern lifted into L.1; the ID-appears-once principle codified (each `SheetId` / `VisualId` / `ParameterName` literal appears at the constructor of the node that owns it — every other reference is a Python variable holding the node ref).

- **L.1 — Tree primitives in `common/tree/`.** Shipped as the `common/tree/` package (split when crossed the 600-line trigger). Full primitive set across 22 substeps:
  - **Structural** — `App` / `Dashboard` / `Analysis` / `Sheet` with parent-child wiring; layout DSL (`sheet.layout.row(height=H).add_<kind>(width=W, ...)` and `sheet.layout.absolute(...)`) constructs + registers + places visuals atomically (eliminates duplicate-placement / unregistered-visual bug classes by construction).
  - **Visuals** — typed subtypes per kind (`KPI` / `Table` / `BarChart` / `Sankey`); `Dim` / `Measure` typed wrappers around `DimensionField` / `MeasureField` with classmethod factories (`Dim.date()`, `Measure.sum()`, `Measure.distinct_count()`, `Column.average()` etc.); `Table.columns` unaggregated mode + `conditional_formatting` passthrough; `BarChart.colors` (stacked-by-X) + axis-label fields + `orientation` / `bars_arrangement` / `sort_by`.
  - **Filters + parameters** — typed `CategoryFilter` / `NumericRangeFilter` / `TimeRangeFilter` wrappers with discriminated-union factories (`CategoryFilter.with_values(...)` / `with_parameter(...)` / `with_literal(...)`; `NumericRangeFilter` `Bound = StaticBound(value) | ParameterBound(parameter)` union); `FilterGroup` with object-ref scope (`sheet.scope(filter_group, [v1, v2])` validates membership at the call site); `StringParam` / `IntegerParam` / `DateTimeParam` declarations; default-control wrappers on Filter wrappers.
  - **Controls** — typed `FilterDropdown` / `FilterSlider` / `FilterDateTimePicker` / `FilterCrossSheet` + `ParameterDropdown` / `ParameterSlider` / `ParameterDateTimePicker` variants wired by object ref into source `FilterGroup` / `ParameterDecl`; sheet shortcuts (`add_filter_dropdown`, `add_parameter_slider`, etc.).
  - **Data + actions** — typed `Dataset` tree nodes (App-level) with `App.dataset_dependencies()` selective dependency graph (drives selective deploy + matview REFRESH ordering, catches "declared but unused" + "used but undeclared" at construction); typed `Column` refs (`ds["column_name"]` validates against `DatasetContract` — `KeyError` at the wiring site on typo); typed `CalcField` tree nodes; typed `Drill` action wrapper (left-click `DATA_POINT_CLICK` / right-click `DATA_POINT_MENU`) with `target_sheet` as a Sheet ref + shape-validated source/destination; `SameSheetFilter` action type for click-to-filter same-sheet patterns.
  - **Auto-IDs** — internal-only IDs (`VisualId`, `FilterGroupId`, `ActionId`, layout element IDs, field-well IDs) auto-resolve at emit time using a position-indexed scheme (`v-{kind}-s{sheet_idx}-{visual_idx}`, `fg-s{sheet_idx}-{idx}`, `f-{visual_kind}-s{sheet_idx}-v{visual_idx}-{role}{slot_idx}`); URL-facing IDs (`SheetId`, `ParameterName`) and analyst-facing identifiers (`Dataset` identifier, `CalcField` name) stay explicit. The `T | AutoResolved` field type + `_AutoSentinel` narrowing means pyright proves the resolver-ran invariant from the field declaration alone — `KPI(visual_id=None)` is now a *type* error at the wiring site.
  - **Type discipline** — pyright strict on `common/tree/` (0 errors) wired into pytest via a `pytest_sessionstart` hook (same gate runs in CI; `QS_GEN_SKIP_PYRIGHT=1` opts out for fast iteration). Locked rule: any new typed-wrapper string field defaults to a `Literal` of QS-allowed values. Runtime `__post_init__` validation reserved for cross-field invariants the type system can't express (mutual-exclusion, registry duplicates, sheet-scope checks).
  - **Test infrastructure** — `TreeValidator(app, page).validate_structure()` typed walker for e2e DOM assertions (per-kind dispatch); `ScreenshotHarness(app, page, output_dir)` typed walker for systematic screenshot capture (three modes: `capture_all_sheets()`, `capture_per_visual()`, `capture_with_state(parameter_values=...)`); kitchen-sink test app exercising every typed primitive at least once; full validator coverage audit (see L.1.18 table — every runtime-raised validator has a dedicated rejection test in the same commit).
  - **Prescriptive API hardening** (L.1.21 + L.1.22 — surfaced during L.2 + L.3 ports) — parent-creates-child API (layout DSL replaced `Sheet.add_visual` + `Sheet.place`; `App.create_dashboard` replaced `App.set_dashboard`; `sheet.scope` reads more naturally than `fg.scope_visuals(sheet, ...)`; sheet shortcuts for control creation) and discriminated-union factory splits (`CategoryFilter.with_values` / `with_parameter`; `NumericRangeFilter` `Bound` union; `LinkedValues.from_column` / `from_string`) — net 10 runtime validators eliminated by construction.
  
  706+ unit tests passing on commit; pyright strict gate at 0 errors. Documented in `CLAUDE.md` "Tree pattern" section + the 7 mkdocstrings-driven API reference pages under `src/quicksight_gen/docs/api/`.

- **L.2 — Port Investigation to the tree.** First port; smallest existing app. Surfaced 4 L.1 friction items that fed back into L.1 (`SheetTextBox` placeable in `GridSlot`; typed `BarChart` `orientation` / `bars_arrangement` / `sort_by` exposure; parameter-bound `CategoryFilter`; `Drill.target_sheet` Optional with auto-fill for same-sheet drills). **Net reduction:** sources 2489 → 1012 lines (`analysis.py` + `filters.py` + `visuals.py` → single `app.py`, **−59%**); tests 1335 → 1442 lines (+8% — added tree-walked helpers); combined **−1370 lines, −36%**. Imperative `apps/investigation/{filters,visuals}.py` (1877 lines) deleted in L.2.13; `tests/test_investigation.py` swapped to tree-walked helpers (`_filter_groups()` reads `build_analysis(cfg).Definition.FilterGroups`, etc.).

- **L.3 — Port Account Reconciliation to the tree.** Largest existing app — 7 sheets including Today's Exceptions / Exceptions Trends / Daily Statement, 14 exception checks, 18 sheet-level filter groups, ~80 visuals; the worst-case stress test for the primitives. New tree extensions surfaced: `Table.columns` unaggregated mode + `conditional_formatting` passthrough; `SameSheetFilter` action type (discriminated `Action = Drill | SameSheetFilter` union); `BarChart.category_label` / `value_label` axis labels; `BarChart.colors` (stacked-by-X); `Dim.date_granularity`; multi-column `Table.sort_by`; default-control wrappers (`DefaultDateTimePickerControl` / `DefaultDropdownControl` / `DefaultSliderControl`); `SelectAllOptions` in `_ValuesBinding`; `TimeEqualityFilter`; `Analysis.find_parameter`; `CategoryFilter.with_literal`. **Net reduction:** sources 3417 → 1933 lines (**−43%**); tests 3428 → 3473 lines (+1.3%); combined **−1439 lines, −21%**. Imperative `apps/account_recon/{analysis,filters,visuals}.py` (3417 lines) deleted in L.3.13; the K.2-invariant test became `test_every_drill_into_transactions_writes_full_param_set`, walking every `Drill` action whose `target_sheet is txn_sheet` and asserting every `_AR_TXN_PASS_FILTERED_PARAMS` entry appears in its writes (catches drill bypasses at the wiring site).

- **L.4 — Port Payment Reconciliation to the tree.** Medium complexity. The Payment Reconciliation tab's mutual-filter pattern (clicking either of two side-by-side detail tables filters the other) wired without needing a dedicated `Sheet.add_mutual_filter_pair(...)` helper — both tables get a same-sheet `Drill` writing the same `pExternalTransactionId` parameter from their row-specific source column. Discovered + fixed a long-standing PR bug in L.4.12a — 6 orphan aging bars (`exceptions-aging-{unsettled,returns,sale-stl-mismatch,stl-pay-mismatch,unmatched-ext}` + `recon-aging-bar`) shipped in `Visuals[]` but were never placed in any `GridLayoutElement`; the new bars wired into Exceptions + Payment Reconciliation rows. **Net reduction:** sources 3343 → 1920 lines (`analysis.py` + `filters.py` + `recon_filters.py` + `visuals.py` + `recon_visuals.py` → single `app.py`, **−43%**); tests 195 → 152 lines (**−22%**); combined **−1466 lines, −41%**. PR shrunk slightly more than AR despite similar complexity because the simpler drill pattern (parameter-bound `CategoryFilter.with_parameter` instead of K.2 PASS calc fields) saved the calc-field plumbing. Imperative `apps/payment_recon/{analysis,filters,recon_filters,visuals,recon_visuals}.py` (3343 lines) deleted in L.4.13.

- **L.6 — Executives app on the new tree from scratch.** Greenfield use as the proving ground that the API works for first-time authors, not just for porting existing apps — the **second iteration gate**. 4 sheets — Getting Started + Account Coverage (counts open + active by `account_type`) + Transaction Volume Over Time (daily count stacked-by-`transfer_type`) + Money Moved (net + gross dollar volume by rail). 2 datasets — `exec_transaction_summary` (per-`(date, transfer_type)` aggregates with per-`transfer_id` pre-aggregation so multi-leg transfers aren't double-counted) + `exec_account_summary` (per-account from `daily_balances` LEFT JOIN'd against an activity rollup). Reuses `default` (non-demo) / `sasquatch-bank` (demo) themes. Cross-app drills (Executives → AR Transactions filtered to `pArAccountId` / `pArTransferType`) **dropped per K.4.7 precedent** — the QS URL-parameter sync defect would leave control widgets showing "All" while data filtered. The L.6 author wrote zero `constants.py` (sheet IDs inline in `app.py`, internal IDs auto-resolved per L.1.16). Greenfield surfaced 3 backlog items: no `LineChart` typed Visual subtype (substituted vertical STACKED bars for daily-trend visuals — same trend signal); visual-scoped filter wiring leaks the `_AutoSentinel` type at the populator's call site (a `Sheet.find_visuals_by_id(*ids)` helper would handle the sentinel internally); no `LinkText` cell-content "click here" CTA when cross-app drills are dropped (the `CustomActionURLOperation` from K.4.7b might carry the workaround).

- **L.7 — Browser e2e for Executives.** 20 new e2e tests across `test_exec_deployed_resources.py`, `test_exec_dashboard_structure.py`, `test_exec_dashboard_renders.py`, `test_exec_sheet_visuals.py` (uses `TreeValidator(exec_app, page).validate_structure()` — one call replaces hand-curated per-sheet visual count + title dicts; tall viewport so Account Coverage's below-the-fold detail table doesn't virtualize). `test_exec_filters.py` skipped (no UI controls — the only filter is the visual-pinned `activity_count >= 1` NumericRangeFilter); `test_exec_drilldown.py` skipped (cross-app drills dropped per L.6.7). Also retired 3 pre-existing structural test debts surfaced during the e2e run: 2 Investigation tests keyed off legacy `V_INV_*` VisualIds (rewrote to walk the tree by visual title; dropped the orphan `V_INV_*` constants); 1 PR `test_all_datasets_declared` over-asserted via fixture (rewrote to derive expected set from `pr_app.dataset_dependencies()`).

- **L.9 — Docs sweep + Python API doc generation.** New `CLAUDE.md` "Tree pattern" + "Three-layer model — L1 / L2 / L3" + "Tree IS the source of truth" sections (with three concrete tree-walking test examples); project-structure tree refreshed (`common/tree/` expanded as 13-submodule package; per-app entries collapsed off dropped `analysis.py` / `visuals.py` / `filters.py` shape into `app.py`-only; `executives/` added). `README.md` "ships three" → "ships four" throughout; new Executives table block + demo scenario block; "Customising" section rewritten to point at `app.py` shape. **mkdocstrings wired** — added `mkdocstrings[python]>=0.26` to docs extras; configured `python` handler with `paths: [src]`, `show_if_no_docstring: true`, `members_order: source`, `signature_crossrefs: true`; created 7 API reference pages under `src/quicksight_gen/docs/api/` (`index.md`, `tree-structure.md`, `tree-visuals.md`, `tree-data.md`, `tree-filters-controls.md`, `tree-actions.md`, `common-foundations.md`); added "API Reference" block to `mkdocs.yml` nav. New customization handbook walkthrough: `walkthroughs/customization/how-do-i-author-a-new-app-on-the-tree.md` (Executives = worked example). `mkdocs build --strict` clean.

- **L.10 — Release as v5.0.2 (major).** Earned by: internal API change (external callers importing `quicksight_gen.apps.*.{analysis,filters,visuals}` for programmatic dashboard construction need to migrate to `quicksight_gen.common.tree`); the new Executives app; the layer-separation cleanup. Per the project's no-backwards-compat-shims rule, no compatibility re-exports of the old per-app builder modules. **Two failed attempts before v5.0.2 shipped clean** — v5.0.0 reached the manual approval gate (TestPyPI publish ran) before being cancelled when the underlying CI run on the same commit was discovered red; v5.0.1 hit a new release-pipeline `tests` gate via two `test_screenshot_harness.py` tests transitively importing playwright (CI's `[dev]` extras don't ship it). v5.0.2 ships the same Phase L work plus three release-pipeline reliability fixes: (a) post-publish install verification on **both** TestPyPI and prod PyPI (each polls `pip install quicksight-gen==<TAG>` 6×30s, runs `--version` check + smoke import of the public surface); (b) `tests` job mirroring `ci.yml`'s pytest+pyright matrix at the start of `release.yml`, with `build` depending on `tests` (any test failure stops the release before any publish step); (c) e2e drilldown collection-time crash fix (`tests/e2e/test_drilldown.py` + `test_ar_drilldown.py` parametrize at module import time before the `QS_GEN_E2E` gate fires — wrap `load_config(None)` to return empty list on `ValueError`) + `screenshot_harness` URL-construction tests skip without playwright via autouse `pytest.importorskip("playwright")` fixture. The "every failed release attempt earns a new version number" policy keeps the publish history honest. v5.0.2 release pipeline ran clean end-to-end (run id 24874497006): tests (3.12 + 3.13) → build → smoke + bake-sample → TestPyPI publish → verify-testpypi-install → manual approval → PyPI publish → verify-pypi-install → GitHub Release. See `RELEASE_NOTES.md`.

- **L.11 — Browser e2e: walk the tree.** Done before L.5 (originally) so layer-separation work would touch less brittle test code; the L.5 deferral made this freestanding rather than a prerequisite. Promoted `pr_app` / `ar_app` / `inv_app` to **session-scoped** fixtures in `tests/e2e/conftest.py` (each builds the App + runs `emit_analysis()` to resolve auto-IDs); module-scoped duplicates removed from the 3 `test_*_dashboard_structure.py` files. Refactored the 3 `test_*_dashboard_renders.py` files to derive `expected = {s.name for s in <app>.analysis.sheets}` instead of carrying hardcoded `EXPECTED_SHEETS` sets. Adopted `TreeValidator(<app>, page).validate_structure()` on the 3 `test_*_sheet_visuals.py` files — one call per file replaces hand-curated per-sheet visual count + title dicts; PR file 105→48 lines, AR 151→52, Investigation 134→61. Filter / parameter control coverage moved to `TreeValidator.validate_sheet_controls(sheet)` (with Cross-Sheet inheritance fallback for control titles). `enumerate_cross_sheet_left_click_drills(app)` collapses `test_drilldown.py` (PR) + `test_ar_drilldown.py` to a single parametrized `test_drill_navigates_to_target_sheet` per file (5 cases derived from the tree match the original hand-curated 5). **Net −118 lines** across changed e2e files; **tightening, not just compaction** (TreeValidator asserts ALL declared visual titles + ALL declared filter/parameter control titles per sheet, where prior tests checked subsets). Adding a new sheet, visual, or control in any tree port now auto-extends test coverage.

**Deferred to Phase M** — L.5 (layer separation: default vs demo overlay) + L.8 (Executives handbook + walkthroughs). Both touch persona/copy surfaces M is rewriting; the L.5 audit findings (Category A always-emitted persona leaks; Category B demo-conditional flavor blocks already gated; Category C already-isolated/intentional) preserved in the active `PLAN.md` for M kickoff. L.6.8's deferral of a `sasquatch-bank-executives` theme preset rolls into M's "unified theme across all 4 dashboards" headline.

**Deploy-gated unchecked substeps** (L.2.11 / L.3.12 / L.4.12 / L.11.6 — full e2e suite runs at planning time) verified end-to-end by the L.10 release pipeline run 24874497006: 184 passing / 9 skipped / 1 xfailed against the deployed 4-app stack.


# PLAN — Phase M (Shipped — v6.0.0+)

# Phase M — Whitelabel-V2 + L2 institutional model → v6.0.0

**Goal.** Land LAYER 2 (institutional model + library) per `SPEC.md`, port AR CMS + PR to L2-as-data as the validation case, then carry the rest of the product (CLI + dashboards + docs + training) along with it. v6.0.0 is the destination.

**Iteration model.** We do NOT know all the steps up front. The plan below sketches key milestones in expected order; each major milestone (M.X) ends with an explicit **iteration gate** where we replan the downstream sub-steps based on what surfaced. SPEC.md gets amended as we discover gaps; PLAN.md sub-steps regenerated. M.4 onward are deliberately sparse — they get fleshed out only after M.3's iteration gate.

**Product surface reminder.** `quicksight-gen` ships four things in lockstep — **CLI + dashboards + docs + training material**. Each milestone should make at least small progress in each area; M.0 is a deliberate full-vertical slice (touches all four minimally) to prove the pipeline shape works before scaling. Subsequent milestones broaden each area.

**L deferrals folded in.** L.5 (layer separation: default vs demo overlay) and L.8 (Executives handbook + walkthroughs) deferred from L land here naturally — both touch the persona/copy surface M is rewriting. Sub-folded into M.7 / M.8 below.

**Testing per-milestone, not deferred.** Each milestone (M.0 spike excepted) explicitly lands its testing surface as the layer is built — Phase L's kitchen-sink + L.1.18 validator-audit pattern carries forward. The rule: every new primitive gets a unit test, every new SPEC validation rule gets a rejection test, every layer gets at least one integration test exercising the layer above's contract, and every L2 instance gets a hash-lock for deterministic seed output. Tests prove the layer is built before we move on; we don't accumulate test debt to clear at M.9. M.0 carries a smoke test only — its job is shape-learning, not coverage; M.4–M.9 placeholders inherit the principle and get specific test sub-steps fleshed out at the iteration gate before each.

- [ ] **M.0 — Vertical-slice spike.** Smallest meaningful end-to-end through CLI → schema → data → dashboard → handbook (with embedded screenshot). Validates the pipeline shape end-to-end before committing to library structure. Same approach as L.0 — surface what works on a tiny case, lift the working primitives into M.1+. Acceptance: a single `quicksight-gen apply --config slice.yaml` + `generate training` flow produces a deployed dashboard showing one drift scenario, plus one rendered handbook page that templates against the L2 instance's vocabulary AND embeds a real screenshot of the deployed dashboard.
  - [x] M.0.1 — Pick scenario. **Decided:** Two-Account Drift Spike — 1 internal account (`int-001`) + 1 external counterparty (`ext-001`); 1 two-leg ach Rail (`ext_inbound`, `ext-001 → int-001`, ExpectedNet=0); 5 inbound transfers of $100 each + a StoredBalance for `int-001` of $450 on the latest day (last transfer didn't make the snapshot → $50 drift). Real Click CLI (minimal but working). Handbook page embeds a real ScreenshotHarness capture of the deployed Drift sheet.
  - [x] M.0.2 — Write `tests/spike/slice.yaml` per the L2 SPEC (1 InstancePrefix, 2 Accounts, 1 Rail; no Templates / Chains / Limits / Aggregating).
  - [x] M.0.3 — Write `src/quicksight_gen/l2_spike/loader.py` — YAML → typed dataclasses + minimal validation (well-formed YAML + required fields present; full SPEC validation lands in M.1).
  - [x] M.0.4 — Write schema SQL emitter (`l2_spike/emit.py::emit_schema_sql`) — emits `<prefix>transactions` + `<prefix>daily_balances` DDL + `<prefix>current_*` views.
  - [x] M.0.5 — Write seed SQL emitter (`l2_spike/emit.py::emit_seed_sql`) — generates 5 ach transfers + 1 drifting StoredBalance row for `int-001`. Deterministic.
  - [x] M.0.6 — Write dashboard emitter (`l2_spike/emit.py::build_dashboard`) — uses `common/tree/` to build 1 sheet "Drift" with 1 KPI + 1 detail table over the prefixed CurrentStoredBalance LEFT JOIN'd against ComputedBalance.
  - [x] M.0.7 — Write handbook templater (`l2_spike/emit.py::render_handbook`) — 1 page "What's a drift exception?" with `{int_account_name}` / `{int_account_id}` substitution sourcing from the loaded L2 instance.

  - [x] M.0.9 — Write `src/quicksight_gen/l2_spike/cli.py` + `__main__.py` — Click commands `apply schema|data|dashboards` + `generate training`. Real CLI (not function stubs); all four commands run end-to-end producing the right artifacts under a fixture cwd.
  - [x] M.0.10 — End-to-end pipeline run against real Postgres + real QuickSight (account 470656905821 / us-east-2). All four CLI commands executed via `--config run/config.yaml`: schema applied, drift seed planted (verified $50 drift via direct SQL), all 5 QuickSight resources deployed (DataSource + Theme + Dataset + Analysis + Dashboard, all `spk-` prefixed), embed URL fetched + Playwright captured a screenshot at `training/spk/drift-sheet.png`, handbook rendered with the substituted account name and resolves to that image. **Lesson captured (F12):** screenshot showed QS's generic "We can't open that dashboard" error because the backing Aurora Serverless Postgres was asleep — DB cold-start is the actual root cause when QS surfaces that error, not permissions / scope. v5.0.2 e2e suite already has a DB warm-up phase; M.7/M.8 must adopt the same pattern.
  - [x] M.0.11 — Write `tests/spike/test_slice.py` — smoke tests: load `slice.yaml`, walk the schema/seed/dashboard/handbook artifacts, assert load-bearing shape; persona substitution check ensures no Sasquatch leakage. 2 tests passing. Full unit suite still green (721 passed).
  - [x] M.0.12 — Findings consolidated in `tests/spike/_l2_spike_findings.md` (12 findings F1-F12). Top-of-file summary buckets them by trigger: SPEC amendment (F5), M.1 library design (F1-F6), refactor touches (F7-F8), confirmations of reusable infra (F9-F11), operational lesson for M.7/M.8 (F12 — DB warm-up).
  - [x] M.0.13 — **Iteration gate.** SPEC amendment landed (F5: InstancePrefix regex `^[a-z][a-z0-9_]*$` + 30-char cap pinned). M.1 substeps below absorb F1-F8 inline; M.7/M.8 absorb F12 (DB warm-up before screenshot). M.0 closed.

- [ ] **M.1 — L2 library foundation.** Lift the spike's working glue into proper library modules. Typed YAML loader matching SPEC; all SPEC validation rules with rejection tests; prefix-aware SQL emission; Current* projection. Acceptance: `from quicksight_gen.l2 import load_instance, validate, ...` works; spike's `slice.yaml` loads through it cleanly; pyright strict on `common/l2/`.
  - [x] M.1.1 — Typed dataclasses landed under `src/quicksight_gen/common/l2/primitives.py` with all SPEC primitives + value types (Account / AccountTemplate / TwoLegRail / SingleLegRail / TransferTemplate / ChainEntry / LimitSchedule / L2Instance) plus enums (Scope / LegDirection) and SPEC-vocabulary type aliases (Origin / TransferType / CompletionExpression / CadenceExpression). Per F2: `Rail = TwoLegRail | SingleLegRail` as a TypeAlias — match-dispatch works without isinstance ladders; aggregating flags live on both shapes per SPEC. All dataclasses `frozen=True, slots=True`. F6 (Dataset rename) deferred to M.1.4 where api `DataSet` usage actually lands. 4 structural regression tests in `tests/test_l2_primitives.py`; full unit suite green at 725 passing.
  - [x] M.1.2 — Loader landed under `src/quicksight_gen/common/l2/loader.py`. `load_instance(path)` reads YAML, dispatches per primitive type, validates per-entity shape, and returns a fully-typed `L2Instance`. Friendly errors cite a logical path (e.g. `accounts[2].id`) + the source file; YAML syntax errors carry PyYAML's native file/line. F4 lands as `_load_money(raw, *, path)` using `Decimal(str(raw))` — preserves '0.1' rather than coercing through float precision. F5 lands as `_load_instance_prefix(raw, *, path)` enforcing `^[a-z][a-z0-9_]*$` + 30-char cap; per the F5 finding, the strict regex applies to InstancePrefix only — other identifiers use a loose non-empty-string check (SPEC's worked examples mix PascalCase Roles + snake_case TransferTypes). Rail discrimination by field-presence (source/destination → TwoLeg; leg_role/leg_direction → SingleLeg; both/neither → reject). RoleExpression normalized to tuple uniformly (single string → 1-tuple). 19 tests in `tests/test_l2_loader.py` covering happy paths (slice.yaml + inline kitchen-sink) + every per-helper rejection. Full unit suite green at 744 passing.
  - [x] M.1.3 — Validator landed under `src/quicksight_gen/common/l2/validate.py`. `validate(instance)` runs 16 cross-entity rules in deterministic order, fail-fast with `L2ValidationError` on the first violation. Rules grouped: U1-U4 (uniqueness on Account.id / AccountTemplate.role / Rail.name / TransferTemplate.name); R1-R6 (reference resolution: rail-touched roles, Account/AccountTemplate.parent_role with template-under-template forbidden per F1, RailNames in TransferTemplate.leg_rails, Chain endpoints, LimitSchedule.parent_role); C1-C2 (≤1 Variable leg per template, XorGroup parent consistency); S1-S6 (the F3 cross-entity ExpectedNet split: standalone two-leg requires expected_net but template-leg forbids it; single-leg reconciliation by Template OR AggregatingRail; aggregating-not-as-Chain.child; aggregating requires cadence + bundles_activity; non-aggregating must NOT carry them); V1-V2 (CompletionExpression + CadenceExpression vocabulary literals per SPEC v1 tables, with bounds checks like monthly-day in 1..31). 50 tests in `tests/test_l2_validate.py` — one rejection per rule plus parametrized vocabulary acceptance/rejection sweeps. Baseline `_baseline_instance()` fixture exercises every primitive shape (and itself passes `validate()`); each test mutates one field via `dataclasses.replace` to trigger one rule. Full unit suite green at 794 passing (was 744; +50).
  - [x] M.1.4 — Schema emitter landed under `src/quicksight_gen/common/l2/schema.py`. `emit_schema(instance)` produces idempotent (drop-then-create) DDL for `<prefix>transactions` + `<prefix>daily_balances` matching the v6 L1 entity shape: `entry BIGSERIAL` per F's Entry primitive; `amount_money` + `amount_direction` split per the L1 Amount invariant (with a Postgres CHECK enforcing sign-direction agreement); `transfer_parent_id` per L1 Transfer.Parent; `expected_eod_balance` + `limits TEXT` (JSON map) on daily_balances. Account fields denormalized onto every row per Implementation Entities (`account_id` / `account_name` / `account_role` / `account_scope` / `account_parent_role`). `Status`, `TransferType`, and `Origin` are open enums with no CHECK so integrators can extend. `metadata TEXT + IS JSON` per the portability constraint; B-tree indexes only (no GIN). DDL verified against real Postgres via psycopg2 — sign-direction CHECK actually rejects positive Debits. 28 unit tests in `tests/test_l2_schema.py` covering prefix isolation, idempotency ordering, every load-bearing column + constraint, denormalized account fields. F9-F11 (existing deploy infra reuse) more naturally lands in M.6 (CLI workflow) than here — M.1.4 is just CREATE TABLE DDL. F6 Dataset rename still deferred — naturally lands when the QS dataset emitter wraps `build_dataset()`. Full unit suite green at 822 passing (was 794; +28). L2 derived tables (account dim, limits dim) deliberately NOT emitted yet — the spike did fine without them; M.2 (porting AR CMS) will surface what's actually needed.
  - [x] M.1.5 — Current* views landed in the same `emit_schema()` script. `<prefix>current_transactions` materializes the L1 CurrentTransaction theorem as `WHERE entry = (SELECT MAX(entry) … WHERE id = tx.id)`; `<prefix>current_daily_balances` materializes CurrentStoredBalance keyed on `(account_id, business_day_start)`. Views drop before tables (Postgres dependency); CREATE after tables. Verified against real Postgres: inserting two rows for the same logical key with different entries produces both in the base table and only the higher-entry row in the view (drift correction works as designed). Combined into emit_schema() rather than a separate emit_views() — integrators get one "apply schema" script. 5 new tests in tests/test_l2_schema.py; full unit suite green at 827 passing (was 822; +5).
  - [x] M.1.6 — Per-primitive end-to-end pipeline tests landed in `tests/test_l2_pipeline.py`. 14 tests walk each SPEC worked-example shape through `load → validate → emit_schema` cleanly: singleton account, AccountTemplate, two-leg standalone Rail, single-leg in TransferTemplate, single-leg Variable-direction, two-leg aggregating, transfer template (parametrized over all 4 Completion vocabulary forms), Chain XOR group, Chain fan-out, LimitSchedule, plus the SPEC's full end-to-end merchant-acquirer example. Doubles as executable SPEC documentation — if a SPEC snippet stops parsing/validating, the named test fires.
  - [x] M.1.7 — Audit cross-reference added to `validate.py` docstring: rule numbering matches `tests/test_l2_validate.py` test names (U1 → `test_u1_*`, etc.). Locked rule documented inline: every new cross-entity validator MUST land its rejection test in the same commit; the rule list in the docstring extends to cover the new validator. The 16-rule list itself IS the audit table — one row per rule with the SPEC justification.
  - [x] M.1.8 — Kitchen-sink fixture landed under `tests/l2/_kitchen.yaml` (~150 lines). Exercises every primitive shape + every variant flag: both rail shapes; aggregating on both shapes; Variable-direction leg; union role; standalone vs template-leg two-leg (covers S1 + S2 sides); two TransferTemplates with different Completion forms; XOR + non-XOR chains; LimitSchedules across multiple roles. Two coverage tests confirm fixture loads cleanly + every primitive kind is reachable. **Surfaced a real SPEC ambiguity (F13):** S3's "single-leg rail must be reconciled" rule was contradicted by the SPEC's own "single-leg aggregating rails permitted (e.g. sweep that lands in external counterparty)" example. Resolved by exempting aggregating single-leg rails from S3 (they ARE the reconciliation mechanism); SPEC + validator + tests amended in this substep. Working as designed — the kitchen-sink fired exactly the kind of integration breakage per-layer tests miss.
  - [x] M.1.9 — `pyproject.toml` `tool.pyright.include` now lists `src/quicksight_gen/common/l2` alongside `common/tree`. Cleared 90 pyright errors → 0: `validate.py` function signatures take `set[Identifier]` instead of `set[str]` (NewType invariance bites at the call sites in `validate()`); `loader.py` centralizes `dict[str, object]` narrowing in two helpers (`_as_mapping` + `_as_list`) so each per-primitive `_load_*` works against precisely-typed mappings instead of the YAML `Any` cascade; dropped unused `_optional` + `T = TypeVar` + `Any` import. Existing `pytest_sessionstart` hook in `conftest.py` (L.1.20 era) auto-picks up the new include — no new test infra; the gate fires before any test on every `pytest` run, matching the `common/tree` gate. 123/123 L2 tests + 844/844 full unit suite green; pyright `0 errors, 1 warning` (the warning is `reportMissingModuleSource` for `yaml` — PyYAML ships no `.py` source the strict mode can index, benign).
  - [x] M.1.10 — Promoted `ScreenshotHarness` + `browser_helpers` from `tests/e2e/` to `src/quicksight_gen/common/browser/` (helpers.py + screenshot.py + __init__.py re-exports). New public surface: `from quicksight_gen.common.browser import ScreenshotHarness, generate_dashboard_embed_url, webkit_page`. Per F8: reshaped harness API to key on object refs — `capture_all_sheets()` now returns `dict[Sheet, Path]`; `capture_per_visual(sheet)` returns `dict[VisualLike, Path]`; `capture_with_state(...)` returns `dict[Sheet, Path]`. On-disk filenames stay `<sheet_id>.png` / `<visual_id>.png` so existing screenshots overwrite cleanly. Spike's `capture_drift_screenshot` rewired (`paths[drift_sheet]` instead of `paths["drift-sheet"]`); 22 e2e test files + 1 unit test + 3 ad-hoc scripts updated to import from the new location. `SCREENSHOT_DIR` resolves relative to cwd (overridable via `QS_E2E_SCREENSHOT_DIR`) so the e2e `screenshot()` helper still writes to `tests/e2e/screenshots/`. CLAUDE.md project-structure tree refreshed (new `common/browser/` block; `tests/e2e/{browser_helpers,screenshot_harness}.py` removed). Common/browser/ deliberately NOT in pyright strict gate yet — `helpers.py` loosely types Playwright Page as plain `page`; tightening queued for when M.6/M.7/M.8 surface real production needs. 844/844 unit tests green; pyright `0 errors`.

- [x] **M.1a — Bring L2 library into alignment with updated SPEC.** Catch-up substep between M.1 and M.2 — the SPEC accumulated changes during the L2-design pass that needed to land in the library before M.2 ports a real app on top. Alignment-only: load-time + data-shape only; runtime mechanics (bundler firing, posting-time PostedRequirements check, aging-watch dashboards, Variable-leg ordering enforcement at posting time) stay deferred to M.2+ where each gets a real caller.
  - [x] M.1a.1 — Schema v1.1 columns + bundler-eligibility index landed (`schema.py`): `rail_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL` + `template_name VARCHAR(100)` + `bundle_id VARCHAR(100)` + `supersedes VARCHAR(50)` on `<prefix>transactions`; `supersedes VARCHAR(50)` on `<prefix>daily_balances`; partial index `idx_<prefix>_transactions_bundler_eligibility ON (rail_name, status) WHERE bundle_id IS NULL`. Open enum on `supersedes` (no CHECK) per SPEC's open-enum rule. Spike's `emit_seed_sql` writes `'ExtInbound'` as `rail_name` per row (single-rail spike); `Current*` views auto-project new columns via `SELECT *`. 7 new tests in `test_l2_schema.py` (851/851 unit suite green).
  - [x] M.1a.2 — L2 primitives v1.1 landed (`primitives.py` + `loader.py`): added `Duration: TypeAlias = datetime.timedelta` + `SupersedeReason: TypeAlias = Literal["Inflight", "BundleAssignment", "TechnicalCorrection"]`. Made `Rail.origin` optional (`Origin | None`); added `posted_requirements: tuple[Identifier, ...]` + `max_pending_age: Duration | None` + `max_unbundled_age: Duration | None` to both `TwoLegRail` + `SingleLegRail`. `TwoLegRail` only: `source_origin: Origin | None` + `destination_origin: Origin | None` (type-level prevents per-leg overrides on `SingleLegRail`). Loader parses new fields including ISO 8601 Duration (`_load_duration` regex handles `PT24H` / `P1D` / `P1DT12H` / etc., rejects year/month/empty/negative/non-string); hard-rejects `source_origin`/`destination_origin` keys on single-leg rails per the M.1a design call. Kitchen-sink fixture exercises every new variant. 8 new primitive tests + 23 new loader tests (882/882 unit suite green).
  - [x] M.1a.3 — Validator catch-up landed (`validate.py`): added 5 new rules — **U5** LimitSchedule (parent_role, transfer_type) uniqueness; **R7** TransferTemplate.leg_rails entries reference non-Aggregating Rails; **R8** MaxUnbundledAge set only on Rails appearing in some AggregatingRail's bundles_activity (bare-identifier selectors match by RailName OR transfer_type); **R9** dotted BundleSelector (`Template.LegRail`) resolves both template + leg-rail (validator does dot-split locally per the bare-identifier-shape design); **O1** per-leg Origin resolution: 1-leg rails MUST set `origin`; 2-leg rails MUST cover both legs via `origin` alone OR both per-leg overrides OR one override + rail-level fallback. Module docstring's audit table updated to document U5/R7/R8/R9/O1; `validate()` wires all five new checks. 14 new rejection + acceptance tests; 64 validator tests total (was 50). Total validator surface: U1–U5, R1–R9, C1–C2, S1–S6, V1–V2, O1 (24 rules). 895/895 unit suite green.
  - [x] M.1a.4 — PostedRequirements computed view landed (`src/quicksight_gen/common/l2/derived.py`). `posted_requirements_for(instance, rail_name) -> tuple[Identifier, ...]` returns the deduped, lex-sorted union of (a) the Rail's own `posted_requirements`, (b) `TransferKey` fields for every TransferTemplate where the rail is in `leg_rails` (handles rails appearing in multiple templates), (c) `parent_transfer_id` (the module-level constant `PARENT_TRANSFER_ID`) when the rail is a Required:true Chain.child OR when a TransferTemplate containing the rail is. `_find_rail` raises `KeyError` on lookup miss. Public API exports `posted_requirements_for` + `PARENT_TRANSFER_ID`. 12 new tests in `test_l2_derived.py` covering each source path independently + combined union + dedup overlap + deterministic sort + lookup miss + chain-parent-not-inheriting. 907/907 unit suite green.
  - [x] M.1a.5 — Committed M.1a.1-4 as one cohesive "M.1a SPEC alignment" commit (`72a479a` on `phase-m-1-l2-library-foundation`). 907/907 unit suite + pyright gate green. Bundled SPEC.md catch-up edits + the planning artifact `M1a_guidance.md` with the implementation so the SPEC + library land in lockstep. (Guidance doc deleted in M.1a.6 — fully absorbed into PLAN + SPEC.)
  - [x] M.1a.6 — Description fields landed on every L2 primitive (`primitives.py` + `loader.py` + `SPEC.md`). Optional `description: str | None = None` on `Account`, `AccountTemplate`, `TwoLegRail`, `SingleLegRail`, `TransferTemplate`, `ChainEntry`, `LimitSchedule`, and top-level `L2Instance`. New `_load_description` helper rejects non-string + blank/whitespace-only values (configuration smell — omit the key instead). Multi-line markdown survives intact (loader does no pre-processing). SPEC.md gained a "Description fields" subsection at the top of `Primitives` documenting the Why (handbook + training render templates read these) and the SHOULD recommendation; each primitive's type signature in SPEC gained the trailing `Description?: Value` field. Kitchen-sink fixture exercises descriptions on top-level instance + Account + AccountTemplate + TwoLegRail + TransferTemplate + ChainEntry + LimitSchedule. M1a_guidance.md deleted (fully absorbed). 13 new tests in `tests/test_l2_descriptions.py`; 920/920 unit suite + pyright gate green.
  - [x] M.1a.7 — L1 invariant views landed in `emit_schema` (`schema.py`). 7 prefixed views per L2 instance materializing the SPEC's L1 SHOULD-constraints as queryable exception surfaces: 2 helper views (`<prefix>_computed_subledger_balance`, `<prefix>_computed_ledger_balance`) + 5 invariant views (`<prefix>_drift`, `<prefix>_ledger_drift`, `<prefix>_overdraft`, `<prefix>_expected_eod_balance_breach`, `<prefix>_limit_breach`). Each invariant view returns ONLY the violation rows. All read from Current* views so technical-error supersession is transparent. Limit-breach caps embedded inline at view-emit time as CASE branches from `instance.limit_schedules` (dynamic JSON path lookup isn't portable across SQL targets); empty `limit_schedules` produces a syntactically valid but inert view. New `_emit_l1_invariant_views(instance)` + `_render_limit_breach_cases(instance, *, p)` helpers. Skipped (deferred to first-consumer): Conservation (transfer-level), Timeliness (transaction-level), Parent-balance-existence (presence check, not value). One existing test fixed (`test_daily_balances_money_is_signed` regex was over-broad — the new `<prefix>_overdraft` view legitimately filters `money < 0`; tightened to look for CHECK on `money` inside the daily_balances CREATE TABLE block specifically). 23 new tests in `test_l2_schema.py` covering each view's DDL shape + filter semantics + parametrized smoke for view existence/drop-create-order across all 7 view names; verified the limit-breach inline CASE branches against a custom L2 fixture. 994/994 unit suite + pyright strict gate green.

- [x] **M.2 — Port AR CMS as first L2 instance feeding the generic L1 dashboard.** **Closed at M.2.10's iteration gate; M.2a takes over.** What shipped: L2 library proven end-to-end against real Aurora (M.2.6 PASS — schema deploys, seed plants, all 3 L1 invariant view scenarios surface). What deferred (subsumed by M.2a): wholesale dataset rewrite under the v5-idiom translation layer (M.2.4c/d), faithful-port handbook page (M.2.5 → M.2a.7), seed hash-lock (M.2.7 → M.2a.8), no-regression run (M.2.8 — M.2a is parallel-stack, both pass independently). Three real bugs surfaced + earned regression tests (cumulative balance semantic, view JOIN that v6 denormalization makes unnecessary, DDL drop ordering). The faithful-port framing got us through enough of the port that the architecture is validated — the L1 invariant views are the right abstraction; M.2a builds on a known-good foundation.
  - [x] M.2.1 — `tests/l2/sasquatch_ar.yaml` landed, exercising every L2 primitive shape the kitchen-sink covers (in different patterns, for variety in regression coverage). 13 singleton accounts (8 internal GL + 5 external sharing role `ExternalCounterparty`); 2 AccountTemplates (`CustomerDDA`/`ZBASubAccount` per R3 singleton-parent); 16 Rails — 6 directional Customer↔External (per-leg origin overrides on inbound, rail-level on outbound), on-us cycle as 3 single-leg rails (one with `Variable` direction) wrapped in a TransferTemplate, ZBASweep + ConcentrationToFRBSweep operational sweeps, ACHOriginationDailySweep (2-leg aggregating, `daily-eod`) + CustomerFeeMonthlySettlement (single-leg aggregating, `monthly-eom`, lands in External per SPEC's permitted exemption), CustomerFeeAccrual (single-leg, union `leg_role: [CustomerDDA, InternalSuspenseRecon]`, `max_unbundled_age: P31D`, bundled by the monthly settlement), 2 ACH return rails (XOR group children); 1 TransferTemplate (`InternalTransferCycle`, `transfer_key: [internal_transfer_id]`, `completion: business_day_end+1d` — different from kitchen-sink's `metadata.<key>`/`business_day_end`); 3 ChainEntries (1 Required:true `ACHOriginationDailySweep → ConcentrationToFRBSweep` for orphan protection + 2 XOR-group `CustomerInboundACH → {NSF, StopPay}` returns); 3 LimitSchedules mirror today's `ar_ledger_transfer_limits`. **Description on every primitive** (top-level instance + every Account, AccountTemplate, Rail, TransferTemplate, ChainEntry, LimitSchedule). Fixture passes the full 24-rule validator clean. 25 smoke tests in `tests/test_l2_sasquatch_ar.py` lock the structural shape M.2.2-M.2.10 will build on AND the new-primitive coverage (TransferTemplate structure, Variable closing leg, two distinct aggregating-rail shapes, single-leg union role, max_unbundled_age, Required:true chain auto-deriving `parent_transfer_id`, XOR-group at-most-one semantics, distinct Completion + Cadence vocabulary forms from kitchen-sink, PostedRequirements derivation across both auto-sources). 945/945 unit suite green; pyright strict gate green.
  - [x] M.2.2 — Seed generator landed at `tests/l2/sasquatch_ar_seed.py` (~430 lines). Public API: `emit_seed(L2Instance, ScenarioPlant) -> str` produces deterministic v6 INSERTs against the prefixed `<prefix>_transactions` + `<prefix>_daily_balances` tables (i.e., the schema M.1.4's `emit_schema` emits). Typed scenario primitives: `TemplateInstance` (concrete materialization of an AccountTemplate; integrator-supplied since the SPEC defers materialization to ETL), `DriftPlant` (delta_money on stored balance vs computed), `OverdraftPlant` (negative money; loader-style validation rejects positive values), `LimitBreachPlant` (outbound debit > LimitSchedule cap). `default_ar_scenario(today)` plants 1 of each scenario kind on 3 customer DDA instances using today's `apps/account_recon/demo_data.py` slugs so cross-checking stays straightforward. Generator output is byte-deterministic (sorted plant order; no random) — pre-requisite for M.2.7's hash-lock. 17 unit tests in `tests/test_l2_seed.py`: smoke (output non-empty, prefixed tables, v1.1 columns); per-scenario shape (drift produces 2 background credits + balance row at $200+delta; overdraft balance < 0 + positive-money rejection; limit-breach 2-leg debit > cap on the right rail/transfer_type); sign-direction agreement on every Debit/Credit row (parallels the schema CHECK); determinism (re-run = byte-identical); multi-plant scenarios; lookup-miss rejection; schema+seed concatenate into a well-formed pipeline. **Real-DB execution + L1 invariant queries surface the planted rows** is M.2.6's integration substep — that's the explicit handoff. 962/962 unit suite + pyright strict gate green.
  - [x] M.2.3 — L2 instance plumbed into the AR build pipeline. New `apps/account_recon/_l2.py` owns `default_l2_instance()` (loads + validates `tests/l2/sasquatch_ar.yaml`); `build_account_recon_app(cfg, *, l2_instance: L2Instance | None = None)` accepts an optional override and auto-loads the default when None. Build shims (`build_analysis`, `build_account_recon_dashboard`) forward the kwarg. `_datasets(cfg, l2_instance)` accepts the instance as a placeholder — M.2.4 will rewrite dataset SQL to use `l2_instance.instance` as the table prefix (`<prefix>_transactions` / `<prefix>_daily_balances`) and replace today's hardcoded `is_internal = TRUE` scope predicates with the v6 `account_scope = 'internal'` form derived from L2 Account roles. **Reframing note:** the original plan wording assumed app.py held hardcoded `account_id` constants to drop — auditing the live app surfaced none (account IDs flow from dataset columns at runtime). M.2.3's real deliverable is the build-time seam M.2.4 consumes; no observable behaviour change. 9 new tests in `tests/test_account_recon_l2_wiring.py` cover the seam (default load, explicit override, kwarg-only signature, backward-compat for kwarg-less callers, build-time validation, prefix availability for M.2.4, account-id alignment with today's `demo_data.py` slugs). 971/971 unit suite + pyright strict gate green.

Connects to the cluster in `run/config.yaml` (Aurora warm-up via `SELECT 1` per F12), applies the v6 schema (~18.5k chars: 2 base tables + Current* views + 7 L1 invariant views + indexes), plants the M.2.2 default scenario, queries each L1 invariant view + asserts each planted scenario surfaces. **3/3 PASS** against `database-1.cluster-c9q0csue47zf.us-east-2.rds.amazonaws.com:5432/postgres`. **Two real bugs surfaced + fixed:** (a) drift view returned 2 rows for the planted account because the seed emitted a $0 baseline daily_balance for today, but L1 SPEC's ComputedBalance is cumulative through end-of-day — fix: drop baseline-today emission, let each scenario plant its own daily_balance(s); (b) limit_breach view JOINed to daily_balances on the breach business_day to look up parent_role, but the seed only planted daily_balance at today (not at breach day) — fix: read parent_role from the transaction row directly (denormalized in v6), no JOIN to daily_balances; (c — found while fixing a + b) schema's L1 view DROPs landed AFTER the Current* DROPs, but the L1 views depend on Current* — fix: emit L1 view DROPs at the top of the script before the base-block DROPs. - [ ] **M.2a — Re-evaluate AR as a generic L1 dashboard.** The framing-shift step. Now that L1 has Status / SupersedeReason / BundleId / aging-watch infrastructure (M.1a), and the AR port (M.2) has proven the L2 plumbing works, ask: what L1-derived visualizations become possible that today's hand-rolled AR didn't have? Rename the dashboard from `<prefix>-ar-dashboard` to `<prefix>-l1-dashboard` (per L2 instance) — the dashboard is L1-driven, fed by L2 to know what to scope; the visualizations are L1 invariants visualized. "AR" as an app concept dissolves; what we have is "L1 dashboard configured by an L2 instance whose persona vocabulary happens to be CMS treasury." Sub-step list deliberately open-ended below — M.2 will surface candidates that bubble up here.
  - [x] M.2a.1 — **Architecture decision: parallel-stack.** New module `apps/l1_dashboard/` builds a fresh tree-built app consuming M.1a.7's L1 invariant views directly. M.2.4a's `_l2_datasets.py` v5-idiom translation becomes a transitional artifact that gets deleted at M.2a's close.
